<h1 class="wp-block-heading has-text-align-center has-x-large-font-size">Interior Design Trends</h1>



<p class="has-text-align-center is-style-text-subtitle is-style-text-subtitle--4" style="font-size:clamp(14px, 0.875rem + ((1vw - 3.2px) * 0.294), 17px);">See the biggest interior design movements shaping 2026 and beyond.</p>



<hr class="wp-block-separator has-alpha-channel-opacity is-style-wide is-style-wide--5" style="margin-top:var(--wp--preset--spacing--30);margin-bottom:var(--wp--preset--spacing--30)"/>

<h3 class="wp-block-heading">Nature as the Primary Design Influence</h3>



<p style="font-size:clamp(0.875rem, 0.875rem + ((1vw - 0.2rem) * 0.196), 1rem);">Natural materials, organic forms, and grounding palettes are guiding design decisions more deeply than ever.&nbsp;</p>
</div>



<div class="wp-block-column is-layout-flow wp-block-column-is-layout-flow">
<figure class="wp-block-image size-full" style="margin-bottom:24px"><img width="1920" height="1080" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=&#039;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#039;%20width=&#039;1920&#039;%20height=&#039;1080&#039;%20viewBox=&#039;0%200%201920%201080&#039;%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="Quiet luxury interior design 2026" class="wp-image-100044 perfmatters-lazy" style="aspect-ratio:4/3;object-fit:cover" data-src="https://sampleboard.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/11/Quiet-luxury-interior-design-2026.avif" data-srcset="https://sampleboard.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/11/Quiet-luxury-interior-design-2026.avif 1920w, https://sampleboard.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/11/Quiet-luxury-interior-design-2026-1116x628.avif 1116w, https://sampleboard.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/11/Quiet-luxury-interior-design-2026-1024x576.avif 1024w, https://sampleboard.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/11/Quiet-luxury-interior-design-2026-500x281.avif 500w, https://sampleboard.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/11/Quiet-luxury-interior-design-2026-768x432.avif 768w, https://sampleboard.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/11/Quiet-luxury-interior-design-2026-1536x864.avif 1536w" data-sizes="(max-width: 1920px) 100vw, 1920px" /></figure>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading">A Return to Quiet, Understated Luxury</h3>



<p style="font-size:clamp(0.875rem, 0.875rem + ((1vw - 0.2rem) * 0.196), 1rem);">Luxury is becoming intimate and understated — defined by craftsmanship, longevity, and materials that settle beautifully with time.</p>
</div>



<div class="wp-block-column is-layout-flow wp-block-column-is-layout-flow">
<figure class="wp-block-image size-full" style="margin-bottom:24px"><img width="1920" height="1080" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=&#039;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#039;%20width=&#039;1920&#039;%20height=&#039;1080&#039;%20viewBox=&#039;0%200%201920%201080&#039;%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="Vintage revival interior design 2026" class="wp-image-100046 perfmatters-lazy" style="aspect-ratio:4/3;object-fit:cover" data-src="https://sampleboard.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/11/Vintage-revival-interior-design-2026.avif" data-srcset="https://sampleboard.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/11/Vintage-revival-interior-design-2026.avif 1920w, https://sampleboard.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/11/Vintage-revival-interior-design-2026-1116x628.avif 1116w, https://sampleboard.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/11/Vintage-revival-interior-design-2026-1024x576.avif 1024w, https://sampleboard.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/11/Vintage-revival-interior-design-2026-500x281.avif 500w, https://sampleboard.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/11/Vintage-revival-interior-design-2026-768x432.avif 768w, https://sampleboard.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/11/Vintage-revival-interior-design-2026-1536x864.avif 1536w" data-sizes="(max-width: 1920px) 100vw, 1920px" /></figure>



<h3 class="wp-block-heading">Nostalgia and Personal Storytelling</h3>



<p style="font-size:clamp(0.875rem, 0.875rem + ((1vw - 0.2rem) * 0.196), 1rem);">People are decorating with emotion, layering their homes with heirlooms, vintage finds, and handcrafted pieces that carry history.</p>
</div>
</div>
</div>

<script id="wp-block-template-skip-link-js-after" type="pmdelayedscript" data-cfasync="false" data-no-optimize="1" data-no-defer="1" data-no-minify="1">
	( function() {
		var skipLinkTarget = document.querySelector( 'main' ),
			sibling,
			skipLinkTargetID,
			skipLink;

		// Early exit if a skip-link target can't be located.
		if ( ! skipLinkTarget ) {
			return;
		}

		/*
		 * Get the site wrapper.
		 * The skip-link will be injected in the beginning of it.
		 */
		sibling = document.querySelector( '.wp-site-blocks' );

		// Early exit if the root element was not found.
		if ( ! sibling ) {
			return;
		}

		// Get the skip-link target's ID, and generate one if it doesn't exist.
		skipLinkTargetID = skipLinkTarget.id;
		if ( ! skipLinkTargetID ) {
			skipLinkTargetID = 'wp--skip-link--target';
			skipLinkTarget.id = skipLinkTargetID;
		}

		// Create the skip link.
		skipLink = document.createElement( 'a' );
		skipLink.classList.add( 'skip-link', 'screen-reader-text' );
		skipLink.id = 'wp-skip-link';
		skipLink.href = '#' + skipLinkTargetID;
		skipLink.innerText = 'Skip to content';

		// Inject the skip link.
		sibling.parentElement.insertBefore( skipLink, sibling );
	}() );
	
//# sourceURL=wp-block-template-skip-link-js-after
</script>
